Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists
==================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on August 12, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim











Do you want to earn two byes for the next Grand Prix you are attending? If so, you can consider participating in the Grand Prix Trials which take place the day before! A total of 30 Modern Grand Prix Trials were held, which means that we have 30 decklists here for your viewing pleasure.


* Marcos Dutra (Titan Shift)
* Luis Guilherme Magalhaes Quiroz (Abzan Company)
* Daniel Caixeta (Amulet Titan)
* Gustavo Augusto Soares (Gifts Storm)
* Fabio Inove (White-Blue Control)
* Leonardo Oliveira (Eldrazi Tron)
* Renan Sim (Ad Nauseam)
* David (Affinity)
* Marcelo Santana (Grishoalbrand)
* Paunillo Santos (Amulet Titan)
* Matheus de Oliveira (Green-White Company)
* Mauro Acerenza (Mardu Burn)
* Celso Fernandes (Eldrazi Tron)
* Alexandre Karin (Affinity)
* Victor Gabriel Carvalho Meira (Abzan Company)
* Kelsen Moura (Red-Green Valakut)
* Pedro Elias Tavares (Gifts Storm)
* Cleon Lemos (Green-White Hatebears)
* Marcelo Miziara (Eldrazi Tron)
* Nicolas Percario (Titan Shift)
* Raul Ramos Amorim (Affinity)
* Filipe Ambrosini (Abzan Company)
* Leo Macklene (Affinity)
* Andre Franco (Titan Shift)
* Eduardo Cabrini (Jeskai Midrange)
* Caio Oleskovice (Grixis Shadow)
* Glauber Teixeira (Living End)
* Pietro Santiago Sales (Titan Shift)
* Jairo Tipple (Death & Taxes)
* Jean Cardoso (Affinity)

Special thanks to the tournament organisers Bazar de Bagdá for their assistance rendered in assembling all this info! With more than 15 archetypes represented, we hope this resource provides an interesting glimpse of the Latin-American metagame! Enjoy!







#### Marcos Dutra’s Titan Shift


#####
